### [1] [When Scaling Fails: Network and Fabric Effects on Distributed GPU Training Performance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04424)
*Dinesh Gopalan,Ratul Ali*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文通过实证研究揭示了大规模分布式GPU训练中网络拓扑、拥塞动态、集体同步和GPU局部性等因素是导致性能扩展失效的关键原因，而非框架或模型层面的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决在实际大规模部署中，随着节点增加出现收益递减和行为不稳定的问题，探究常被高层训练框架忽视的网络和硬件架构影响。

Method: 在多个生产级集群上对分布式GPU训练性能进行实证研究，分析不同网络拓扑、运行时通信模式及工作负载下的表现差异。

Result: 发现网络拓扑、拥塞动态、集体同步行为和GPU局部性主导了端到端训练性能；同一模型和软件栈在不同硬件设计下表现出截然不同的扩展特性；识别出同步放大、拓扑诱导竞争和局部性驱动的性能波动等常见故障模式。

Conclusion: 这些效应通常被标准性能分析工具忽略，导致误诊；文章提出了实用的诊断原则，帮助系统构建者理解扩展限制、提高可预测性并降低大规模分布式训练成本。

Abstract: Scaling distributed GPU training is commonly assumed to yield predictable performance gains as additional nodes are added. In practice, many large-scale deployments encounter diminishing returns and unstable behavior well before theoretical limits are reached. This paper examines why scaling fails in real systems, with a focus on the role of network and fabric effects that are often overlooked by higher-level training frameworks. We present an empirical study of distributed GPU training performance across multiple production-scale clusters. Our results show that network topology, congestion dynamics, collective synchronization behavior, and GPU locality frequently dominate end-to-end training performance once workloads move beyond a small number of nodes. Identical models and software stacks can exhibit sharply different scaling characteristics depending on fabric design and runtime communication patterns. We identify recurring failure modes that emerge as training transitions from single-node to multi-node execution, including synchronization amplification, topology-induced contention, and locality-driven performance variance. These effects are often invisible to standard profiling tools and are therefore misdiagnosed as framework or model-level inefficiencies. Based on these findings, we outline practical diagnostic principles that system builders can apply to understand scaling limits, improve predictability, and reduce the cost of large-scale distributed training.

</details>


### [2] [Data-Driven Optimization of Multi-Generational Cellular Networks: A Performance Classification Framework for Strategic Infrastructure Management](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04425)
*Maryam Sabahat,M. Umar Khan*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文基于OpenCelliD项目数据，分析了1818个蜂窝基站（主要为LTE）在三个国家（以巴基斯坦为主）的部署、利用及基础设施缺口，揭示了2G/3G网络长期存在、大量基站利用率不足以及“非4G需求区”等问题，并提出信号密度指标区分过度使用和局部拥塞，为运营商提供LTE升级和资源优化建议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 移动数据需求的指数级增长亟需智能管理电信基础设施，以确保服务质量(QoS)和运营效率。

Method: 对来自OpenCelliD项目的多代蜂窝网络数据集进行地理、时间和性能分析，涵盖1,818个基站条目，主要关注LTE技术，分布在三个国家（巴基斯坦占主导）。研究引入了信号密度指标来区分绝对过载和局部拥塞。

Result: 发现主要城市中心长期保留遗留的2G/3G基础设施；存在大量利用率不足的基站，具有成本节约潜力；识别出特定“非4G需求区”，即活跃用户群仍由过时技术提供服务；通过信号密度指标成功区分了绝对过载与局部拥塞。

Conclusion: 研究结果为移动网络运营商(MNOs)提供了可操作的情报，指导其制定战略性的LTE升级计划、优化资源配置，并弥合欠发达地区的数字鸿沟。

Abstract: The exponential growth in mobile data demand necessitates intelligent management of telecommunications infrastructure to ensure Quality of Service (QoS) and operational efficiency. This paper presents a comprehensive analysis of a multigenerational cellular network dataset, sourced from the OpenCelliD project, to identify patterns in network deployment, utilization, and infrastructure gaps. The methodology involves geographical, temporal, and performance analysis of 1,818 cell tower entries, predominantly Long Term Evolution (LTE), across three countries with a significant concentration in Pakistan. Key findings reveal the long-term persistence of legacy 2G/3G infrastructure in major urban centers, the existence of a substantial number of under-utilized towers representing opportunities for cost savings, and the identification of specific "non-4G demand zones" where active user bases are served by outdated technologies. By introducing a signal-density metric, we distinguish between absolute over-utilization and localized congestion. The results provide actionable intelligence for Mobile Network Operators (MNOs) to guide strategic LTE upgrades, optimize resource allocation, and bridge the digital divide in underserved regions.

</details>


### [3] [Arterial Network Traffic State Prediction with Connected Vehicle Data: An Abnormality-Aware Spatiotemporal Network](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04432)
*Lei Han,Mohamed Abdel-Aty,Yang-Jun Joo*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 提出一种基于真实网联车辆(CV)数据的大规模干线网络交通预测框架，包含两阶段状态提取方法和异常感知时空图卷积网络(AASTGCN)，有效解决了现有研究局限于仿真或小规模网络的难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于CV的干线交通测度预测研究多局限于高渗透率的仿真场景或小型网络，难以直接应用于现实世界的大规模城市干线网络，存在实际落地应用的鸿沟。

Method: 1. 构建两阶段交通状态提取方法：从CV轨迹估算车辆级交通测度，并聚合为网络级交通状态测度；2. 设计异常感知时空图卷积网络(AASTGCN)，采用双专家架构分别建模正常与异常交通流，结合带门控融合机制的时空GCN，同时捕捉短期动态和长期周期性。

Result: 在包含1,050个路段的大型干线网络上使用真实CV数据验证：(1) 提出的状态提取方法能有效提供实时链路级平均延误和排队长度等关键指标；(2) AASTGCN通过分离建模异常与正常交通，在两种工况下的预测性能均优于现有模型；(3) 门控融合机制能自适应平衡实时信息与历史信息，正常工况侧重历史周期性，异常突变工况侧重实时动态。

Conclusion: 该框架成功利用真实世界CV数据实现了大规模干线网络的高效交通状态估计与预测，特别是通过双专家架构和自适应门控机制显著提升了异常交通条件下的预测精度，为城市交通运行与管理提供了可靠的技术支持。

Abstract: Emerging connected-vehicle (CV) data shows great potential in urban traffic monitoring and forecasting. However, prior CV-based studies on arterial traffic measures prediction are limited to simulated high-penetration scenarios or small networks, which are challenging to apply in real-world city-scale arterial networks. To address such gaps, we develop a CV data-based arterial traffic prediction framework with two components: (1) a two-stage traffic state extraction method that estimates vehicle-level traffic measures from CV trajectories and then aggregates them into network-level traffic state measures; (2) an Abnormality-aware spatiotemporal graph convolution network (AASTGCN) that adopts a dual-expert architecture to separately model normal and abnormal traffic, and jointly captures short-term traffic dynamics and long-term periodicity via spatiotemporal GCN with a gated-fusion mechanism. Real-world CV data are used to test our method in a large arterial network with 1,050 links. Experimental results show that: 1) The proposed traffic estimation method is effective for large arterial networks to provide real-time traffic measures (e.g., link-level average travel delay and queue length), which are critical for urban traffic operation and evaluation. 2) Abnormal traffic prediction is typically challenging for existing methods. By modeling abnormal cases separately from normal traffic in two dedicated experts, AASTGCN outperforms existing models for both normal and abnormal traffic conditions. 3) The gate-fusion mechanism adaptively balances real-time and historical information: it leverages more historical-periodic information in normal traffic and shifts a higher weight to real-time traffic dynamics for abnormal traffic deviating abruptly from historical patterns.

</details>


### [4] [Auction-Based RIS Allocation With DRL: Controlling the Cost-Performance Trade-Off](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04433)
*Martin Mark Zan,Stefan Schwarz*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 论文研究多小区无线网络中可重构智能表面（RIS）的分配问题，提出基于同时递增拍卖和深度强化学习（DRL）的动态租赁机制。基站通过宏观信道参数评估效用，利用DRL优化竞价行为，在预算约束下实现成本与频谱效率的最优平衡。仿真表明，该方法优于启发式策略，并引入可调参数灵活控制网络性能与支出的权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多小区无线网络中，独立运营商部署的RIS单元需高效分配给竞争控制的基站。传统静态分配难以适应动态需求，而现有竞价机制缺乏对复杂网络环境和预算约束的自适应能力，导致资源利用率低或成本过高。因此，需要一种可扩展、低开销且能动态优化RIS分配的机制。

Method: 提出一种基于同时递增拍卖格式的动态租赁机制：1) 基站利用宏观信道参数估算获取额外RIS的效用；2) 集成深度强化学习（DRL）代理，使其在预算约束下学习最大化性能的竞价策略；3) 设计可调参数以控制DRL代理的竞价激进程度，调节性能与成本的权衡；4) 在聚类小区边缘环境中进行仿真验证。

Result: 仿真结果显示，基于强化学习的竞价策略显著优于启发式策略，实现了成本与频谱效率之间的最优权衡。引入的可调参数成功控制了代理的竞价行为，使系统能在不同场景下灵活平衡网络性能与支出。该方法证明了拍卖机制与自适应RL结合在提升RIS利用效率方面的潜力。

Conclusion: 将拍卖式分配与自适应强化学习机制相结合，可有效实现下一代无线网络中RIS的高效、公平利用。该框架具备可扩展性、低开销特性，并能通过参数调整灵活适应不同网络条件，为未来动态资源管理提供了新范式。

Abstract: We study the allocation of reconfigurable intelligent surfaces (RISs) in a multi-cell wireless network, where base stations compete for control of shared RIS units deployed at the cell edges. These RISs, provided by an independent operator, are dynamically leased to the highest bidder using a simultaneously ascending auction format. Each base station estimates the utility of acquiring additional RISs based on macroscopic channel parameters, enabling a scalable and low-overhead allocation mechanism. To optimize the bidding behavior, we integrate deep reinforcement learning (DRL) agents that learn to maximize performance while adhering to budget constraints. Through simulations in clustered cell-edge environments, we demonstrate that reinforcement learning (RL)-based bidding significantly outperforms heuristic strategies, achieving optimal trade-offs between cost and spectral efficiency. Furthermore, we introduce a tunable parameter that governs the bidding aggressiveness of RL agents, enabling a flexible control of the trade-off between network performance and expenditure. Our results highlight the potential of combining auction-based allocation with adaptive RL mechanisms for efficient and fair utilization of RISs in next-generation wireless networks.

</details>


### [5] [Periodic Scheduling of Grouped Time-Triggered Signals on a Single Resource](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04434)
*Josef Grus,Zdeněk Hanzálek,Claire Hanen*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文研究了时间触发信号分组为消息及在单资源上进行周期性调度的基本问题，旨在解决信号分组中的效率与约束平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在现代通信网络（如汽车和航空电子领域）中，时间触发消息对于实现确定性行为至关重要。虽然将多个短信号组合成单个消息可以减少头部元数据的开销并提高带宽利用率，但信号分组面临消息最大尺寸限制、长消息传输成功率降低以及调度灵活性下降等复杂挑战。

Method: 研究将时间触发信号分组到消息中，并在单一资源上对这些消息进行周期性调度的基础问题，探索信号分组策略与调度算法的协同优化。

Result: 提出了针对信号分组与周期性消息调度的解决方案框架，解决了如何在有限消息尺寸和调度灵活性约束下，优化通信资源利用率的问题。

Conclusion: 通过有效结合信号分组策略与周期性调度机制，可以在保证消息传输可靠性和调度灵活性的同时，显著提升通信资源的利用效率，满足关键应用对确定性行为的严格要求。

Abstract: Time-triggered messages are of crucial importance in modern communication networks. Offline-generated schedules, which specify start times for periodic messages, enable us to achieve deterministic behavior in critical applications. In automotive and avionics domains, so-called signals (measurements and commands) are periodically generated and communicated (via messages) among sensors, controllers, and actuators. However, the message contains not only the useful signal data, but also necessary metadata, e.g., message ID. Metadata is stored as a header or tail and extends the message size; when the signal is very short (as it often is in applications), sending each in a separate message is inefficient. Thus, several signals are grouped into a single message, depending on their periodicity and length, and sent with just one header. Such an approach increases the utilization of the communication resource (link or bus), since less bandwidth is wasted on headers (Kuaban et al. 2021). However, grouping the signals into messages is complicated. The maximum size of the message (including the metadata) is finite, since longer messages have a lower probability of successful delivery. Also, longer messages are less flexible for scheduling in a periodic setting. This is similar to the work of Huan et al. (2019), where the compromise between energy efficiency and latency for IoT devices was investigated. In this paper, we study the fundamental problem of grouping time-triggered signals into messages and periodic scheduling of messages on a single resource.

</details>


### [6] [Energy Efficiency Testing and Modeling of a Commercial O-RAN System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04435)
*N. K. Shankaranarayanan,Akash Gupta,Zhuohuan Li,Sarat Puthenpura,Jens Sohn,Ivan Seskar,Sreenidhi Parthasarathy,Wilfred Luiz,Jeffrey Williamson,VenkataReddy Varra,Prasanthi Maddala,Alex Stancu*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文基于商用O-RAN系统的实测数据，建立了能量消耗模型，识别了影响功耗的关键因素，为运营商优化能源效率提供数据支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 网络能效对移动运营商至关重要，但缺乏商用O-RAN系统组件及系统层面的定量能耗数据和行为特征描述，难以实现最大化的节能收益。

Method: 通过ORCID实验室与Open Networking Foundation/Rutgers WINLAB的联合项目，在复现生产环境的测试场中，对包含AWS托管O-CU、专用服务器O-DU及6个多频段O-RU的商用O-RAN系统进行全面的功率和性能测量。

Result: 识别了O-RAN协议栈中影响功耗的主导因素，量化了不同操作和流量场景下的能耗变化，并提供了可参数化功耗模型的实测数据。

Conclusion: 这些测量结果为运营商提供了数据驱动的能源优化依据，有助于实现商业O-RAN网络的可持续运营和更高能效。

Abstract: Network energy efficiency is of critical importance to mobile network operators for economic and ecological reasons. The advent of the O-RAN architecture has brought disaggregation and virtualization, and in order to achieve the highest energy savings gains, we need rigorous measurement, analysis, and modeling of energy consumption at both the component and system levels. However, there remains a lack of publicly-available, quantitative data characterizing the behavior of commercial-grade O-RAN systems. In this white paper, we present a detailed energy-efficiency characterization and modeling of a commercial O-RAN system based on comprehensive power and performance measurements, using a network deployment that faithfully replicates a production O-RAN network deployed by a wireless carrier. The results are drawn from an energy test campaign conducted through a joint collaboration between the Open RAN Center for Integration and Deployment (ORCID) Lab Testing and Evaluation (T&E) Project and the Open Networking Foundation / Rutgers WINLAB Energy Efficiency R&D project. The test environment includes an O-RAN system with an AWS-hosted O-CU, a dedicated-server O-DU, and six high-power, multi-band O-RUs. Our results identify the dominant factors influencing power consumption across the O-RAN stack and quantify energy usage variation under different operational and traffic scenarios. These measurements can be used by operators to parameterize power-consumption models, ultimately supporting data-driven energy optimization and more sustainable operation of commercial O-RAN networks.

</details>


### [7] [Towards Green Connectivity: An AI-Driven Mesh Architecture for Sustainable and Scalable Wireless Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04442)
*Muhammad Ahmed Mohsin,Muhammad Jazib,Muhammad Saad,Ayesha Mohsin*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 提出一种基于AI的网状网络架构，通过近距离节点部署、空间频率复用和预测性智能，解决传统宏/微蜂窝网络能效低（<5%）和高密度场景（如朝觐）下的高能耗、高排放及高故障率问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有宏/微蜂窝基础设施能效极低（不到5%），导致95%的射频功率浪费；在高密度临时场景（如朝觐）中，依赖柴油发电塔不仅消耗巨大燃料（年5600万升）、排放大量CO2（14.8万吨），且峰值需求下故障率高达40%，亟需可持续、高效的替代方案。

Method: 提出三种集成使能技术：(i) 基于用户距离250-300米的近距离低功耗节点部署，获得38 dB链路预算增益；(ii) 空间频率复用，将小区划分为多个非干扰区域以实现容量提升；(iii) 利用LSTM进行5秒前向交通流量预测，实现智能资源分配。结合传播建模和链路预算分析进行系统级评估。

Result: 该架构实现了84倍的有用能量传输效率提升，部署成本降低约74%，通过太阳能供电消除对柴油的依赖；同时获得6000倍能效改进、近20倍容量增益，并将拥塞减少约60%。

Conclusion: 所提出的AI驱动网状架构为农村和超密集城市环境提供了可持续、绿色的连接解决方案，显著提升了能效、降低了成本和碳排放，并增强了网络可靠性。

Abstract: Traditional macro-cell and micro-cell infrastructures suffer from severe inefficiencies, with current macro-cell networks operating at less than 5 percent energy efficiency, leading to nearly 95 percent of RF power wasted in covering vacant areas. The problem becomes particularly acute in high-density scenarios such as the Hajj, where approximately 7,000 temporary diesel-powered towers are deployed each year, consuming 56 million liters of fuel and emitting around 148,000 tons of CO2, yet still experiencing failure rates of nearly 40 percent at peak demand. To overcome these limitations, we propose an AI-driven mesh architecture based on three integrated enablers: (i) proximity-based deployment of low-power nodes within 250 to 300 meters of users, yielding a 38 dB link-budget gain and up to 6000 times efficiency improvement; (ii) spatial frequency reuse, which partitions cells into multiple non-interfering zones and achieves nearly 20 times capacity gain; and (iii) predictive network intelligence leveraging LSTMs to forecast traffic 5 seconds ahead, enabling smarter allocation and reducing congestion by about 60 percent. System-level evaluations combining propagation modeling and validated link-budget analysis demonstrate that this architecture delivers up to an 84 times improvement in useful energy delivery, reduces deployment costs by nearly 74 percent, and eliminates diesel dependence through solar-powered operations, thereby enabling sustainable, green connectivity for both rural and ultra-dense urban environments.

</details>


### [8] [vLLM Semantic Router: Signal Driven Decision Routing for Mixture-of-Modality Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04444)
*Xunzhuo Liu,Huamin Chen,Samzong Lu,Yossi Ovadia,Guohong Wen,Zhengda Tan,Jintao Zhang,Senan Zedan,Yehudit Kerido,Liav Weiss,Bishen Yu,Asaad Balum,Noa Limoy,Abdallah Samara,Brent Salisbury,Hao Wu,Ryan Cook,Zhijie Wang,Qiping Pan,Rehan Khan,Avishek Goswami,Houston H. Zhang,Shuyi Wang,Ziang Tang,Fang Han,Zohaib Hassan,Jianqiao Zheng,Avinash Changrani*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: vLLM Semantic Router 是一个信号驱动的决策路由框架，用于在混合模态（MoM）模型部署中智能选择最合适的模型。它通过组合异构信号和可配置的布尔规则，实现针对不同场景（如多云、隐私合规、成本优化等）的灵活路由策略，而无需修改代码。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大型语言模型（LLMs）在模态、能力和成本上的多样化，如何在推理时针对每个查询选择最合适的模型（即智能请求路由）已成为关键的系统挑战。现有的单一模型难以同时满足多样化的业务需求，需要一种能够动态适配不同部署场景的路由机制。

Method: 提出了一种“可组合的信号编排”核心创新：从请求中提取异构信号（包括毫秒级启发式特征如关键词、语言检测、上下文长度，以及神经网络分类器如领域、嵌入相似度等），并通过可配置的布尔决策规则将其组合成特定于部署的路由策略。系统还集成了多种选择算法以优化成本效益，并通过插件链执行隐私和安全约束（如越狱检测、PII过滤、HaluGate三阶段幻觉检测）。架构上支持OpenAI API，具备多端点、多提供商路由能力，并作为Envoy外部处理器在生产环境中部署。

Result: 该框架成功实现了单一路由架构服务于多样化部署场景的能力，能够根据具体需求差异化地处理成本、隐私和安全策略。实验表明，该系统能够在不改变代码的情况下，适应多云企业、隐私监管、成本优化和延迟敏感等多种场景，有效驱动语义模型路由。

Conclusion: vLLM Semantic Router 证明了可组合的信号编排是解决多模态模型智能路由问题的有效途径。它提供了一个高度灵活、可扩展且生产就绪的解决方案，使得复杂的混合模型部署能够通过配置而非硬编码来满足不同业务对成本、隐私和安全的差异化要求。

Abstract: As large language models (LLMs) diversify across modalities, capabilities, and cost profiles, the problem of intelligent request routing -- selecting the right model for each query at inference time -- has become a critical systems challenge. We present vLLM Semantic Router, a signal-driven decision routing framework for Mixture-of-Modality (MoM) model deployments.
  The central innovation is composable signal orchestration: the system extracts heterogeneous signal types from each request -- from sub-millisecond heuristic features (keyword patterns, language detection, context length, role-based authorization) to neural classifiers (domain, embedding similarity, factual grounding, modality) -- and composes them through configurable Boolean decision rules into deployment-specific routing policies. Different deployment scenarios -- multi-cloud enterprise, privacy-regulated, cost-optimized, latency-sensitive -- are expressed as different signal-decision configurations over the same architecture, without code changes.
  Matched decisions drive semantic model routing: over a dozen of selection algorithms analyze request characteristics to find the best model cost-effectively, while per-decision plugin chains enforce privacy and safety constraints (jailbreak detection, PII filtering, hallucination detection via the three-stage HaluGate pipeline).
  The system provides OpenAI API support for stateful multi-turn conversations, multi-endpoint and multi-provider routing across heterogeneous backends (vLLM, OpenAI, Anthropic, Azure, Bedrock, Gemini, Vertex AI), and a pluggable authorization factory supporting multiple auth providers. Deployed in production as an Envoy external processor, the architecture demonstrates that composable signal orchestration enables a single routing framework to serve diverse deployment scenarios with differentiated cost, privacy, and safety policies.

</details>


### [9] [Dynamic Model Routing and Cascading for Efficient LLM Inference: A Survey](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04445)
*Yasmin Moslem,John D. Kelleher*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文系统分析了针对独立大语言模型（LLM）的动态路由与级联方法，提出一个包含决策时机、信息利用和计算方式的三维概念框架，指出有效路由需平衡效率与性能，并强调实际系统常为多种范式的组合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着具备不同能力、成本和领域的LLM快速增长，推理时智能选择模型的需求日益迫切。静态部署无法根据查询的复杂度和领域自适应调整，导致性能次优且成本增加，亟需能够根据查询特征自适应选择模型的动态路由系统。

Method: 对最先进的多LLM路由和级联方法进行系统性分析，涵盖查询难度、人类偏好、聚类、不确定性量化、强化学习、多模态及级联等多种范式；对比混合专家架构，聚焦于跨多个独立训练LLM的路由策略；构建包含“何时决策”、“使用何种信息”及“如何计算”三个维度的概念框架以表征路由系统。

Result: 分析表明，有效的多LLM路由需要在相互竞争的目标之间取得平衡；最优路由策略取决于具体的部署环境和计算约束；设计良好的路由系统能通过战略性地利用各模型的特化能力并最大化效率增益，其表现甚至优于单一最强模型；目前仍面临在多样化架构、模态和应用中实现通用路由机制的挑战。

Conclusion: 实践中的路由系统通常是组合式的，需整合多种范式以适应运营约束；未来研究应致力于开发能泛化至不同架构、模态和应用的通用路由机制，以在多LLM生态中实现性能与效率的最佳平衡。

Abstract: The rapid growth of large language models (LLMs) with diverse capabilities, costs, and domains has created a critical need for intelligent model selection at inference time. While smaller models suffice for routine queries, complex tasks demand more capable models. However, static model deployment does not account for the complexity and domain of incoming queries, leading to suboptimal performance and increased costs. Dynamic routing systems that adaptively select models based on query characteristics have emerged as a solution to this challenge.
  We provide a systematic analysis of state-of-the-art multi-LLM routing and cascading approaches. In contrast to mixture-of-experts architectures, which route within a single model, we study routing across multiple independently trained LLMs. We cover diverse routing paradigms, including query difficulty, human preferences, clustering, uncertainty quantification, reinforcement learning, multimodality, and cascading. For each paradigm, we analyze representative methods and examine key trade-offs. Beyond taxonomy, we introduce a conceptual framework that characterizes routing systems along three dimensions: when decisions are made, what information is used, and how they are computed. This perspective highlights that practical systems are often compositional, integrating multiple paradigms under operational constraints.
  Our analysis demonstrates that effective multi-LLM routing requires balancing competing objectives. Choosing the optimal routing strategy depends on deployment and computational constraints. Well-designed routing systems can outperform even the most powerful individual models by strategically leveraging specialized capabilities across models while maximizing efficiency gains. Meanwhile, open challenges remain in developing routing mechanisms that generalize across diverse architectures, modalities, and applications.

### [10] [Threadle: A Memory-Efficient Network Storage and Query Engine for Large, Multilayer, and Mixed-mode Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04446)
*Carl Nordlund,Yukun Jiao*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: Threadle 是一个用 C# 编写的高性能、内存高效的开源网络存储与查询引擎，专为处理基于行政登记数据的全人口网络（包含数百万节点和数十亿边）而设计。其核心创新在于“伪投影”方法，允许在不实际生成内存消耗巨大的单模投影的情况下，将双模（二分）数据作为单模形式进行查询。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的网络库无法高效地大规模处理双模（二分）数据，这限制了全人口规模、多层、混合模式网络的分析能力。需要一种能够处理包含数百万节点和数十亿边的超大规模网络的解决方案。

Method: 提出了一种“伪投影”（pseudo-projection）的核心算法，使得双模层可以在不物化（materialize）内存禁止的投影的情况下被查询为单模形式。此外，提供了原生的多层混合模式网络支持、集成的节点属性管理器以及包含50多个命令的命令行界面（CLI）。

Result: 实验证明，Threadle 可以将包含2000万个节点且等效于8万亿条投影边的网络存储在约20 GB的RAM中，与物化投影相比压缩比超过2000:1。同时开发了配套的R语言前端 threadleR，支持在超大规模异构网络上进行高级采样和遍历分析。

Conclusion: Threadle 有效解决了现有工具在处理大规模双模网络时的内存瓶颈问题，通过创新的伪投影技术实现了极高的存储效率，为全人口规模的复杂网络分析提供了可扩展的开源基础架构。

Abstract: We present Threadle, an open-source, high-performance, and memory-efficient network storage and query engine written in C#. Designed for working with full-population networks derived from administrative register data, which represent very large, multilayer, mixed-mode networks with millions of nodes and billions of edges, Threadle addresses a fundamental limitation of existing network libraries: the inability to efficiently handle two-mode (bipartite) data at scale. Threadle's core innovation is a pseudo-projection approach that allows two-mode layers to be queried as if they were projected into one-mode form, without ever materializing the memory-prohibitive projection. We demonstrate that a network with 20 million nodes containing layers equivalent to 8 trillion projected edges can be stored in approximately 20 GB of RAM -- a compression ratio exceeding 2000:1 compared to materialized projection. Additionally, Threadle provides native support for multilayer mixed-mode networks, an integrated node attribute manager, and a CLI frontend with 50+ commands for the construction, processing, file handling, and management of very large heterogeneous networks. Threadle is freely available at https://www.threadle.dev and can either be obtained as precompiled binaries for Win, macOS and Linux, or compiled directly from source. Supplementing Threadle is threadleR, an R frontend that enables advanced sampling- and traversal-based analyses on very large, heterogeneous, multilayer, mixed-mode population-scale networks.

</details>

Method: 构建了一个分布式拍卖框架，其中每个基站独立进行多信道拍卖，用户设备（UE）自主决定关联基站和出价策略。在该框架下，UE面临预算约束和重复互动，被建模为长期经济决策问题。研究比较了经典短视/贪婪策略与具备历史推理、竞争预测及策略适应能力的LLM智能体的表现。

While auction-based mechanisms have been widely employed for efficient resource allocation, most prior works assume one-shot auctions, static bidder behavior, and idealized conditions. In contrast to traditional formulations where base station (BS) association and power allocation are centrally optimized, we propose a distributed auction-based framework in which each BS independently conducts its own multi-channel auction, and user equipments (UEs) strategically decide both their association and bid values. Within this setting, UEs operate under budget constraints and repeated interactions, transforming resource allocation into a long-term economic decision rather than a one-shot optimization problem. The proposed framework enables the evaluation of diverse bidding behaviors -from classical myopic and greedy policies to LLM-based agents capable of reasoning over historical outcomes, anticipating competition, and adapting their bidding strategy across episodes. Simulation results reveal that the LLM-empowered UE consistently achieves higher channel access frequency and improved budget efficiency compared to benchmarks. These findings highlight the potential of reasoning-enabled agents in future decentralized wireless networks markets and pave the way for lightweight, edge-deployable LLMs to support intelligent resource allocation in next-generation HetNets.

*Zongyuan Zhang,Tianyang Duan,Liang Wang,Zihan Fang,Zheng Lin,Yijun Lu,Jiening Wu,Xia Du,Miao Yang,Zhe Chen,Heming Cui,Jun Luo*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 边缘设备AI应用激增需要高效的多路径传输协议；现有Multipath TCP的在核拥塞控制缺乏可编程性，且网络状态部分可观测（存在测量噪声）阻碍了数据驱动方法的应用。

Method: 设计解耦架构：轻量级内核客户端与用户空间代理分离控制决策至外部决策引擎；采用基于Transformer的DRL智能体，利用自注意力机制捕捉时间依赖、过滤噪声并协调子流控制策略。

Result: 在模拟环境和真实双频Wi-Fi测试床上的广泛评估表明，TCCO相比最先进基线具有更优越的适应性和性能表现。

Abstract: The proliferation of artificial intelligence applications on edge devices necessitates efficient transport protocols that leverage multi-homed connectivity across heterogeneous networks. While Multipath TCP enables bandwidth aggregation, its in-kernel congestion control mechanisms lack the programmability and flexibility needed for achieving efficient transmission. Additionally, inherent measurement noise renders network state partially observable, challenging data-driven approaches like deep reinforcement learning (DRL). To address these challenges, we propose a Transformer-based Congestion Control Optimization (TCCO) framework for multipath transport. TCCO employs a decoupled architecture that offloads control decisions to an external decision engine via a lightweight in-kernel client and user-space proxy, enabling edge devices to leverage external computational resources while maintaining TCP/IP compatibility. The Transformer-based DRL agent in the external decision engine uses self-attention to capture temporal dependencies, filter noise, and coordinate control across subflows through a unified policy. Extensive evaluation on both simulated and real dual-band Wi-Fi testbeds demonstrates that TCCO achieves superior adaptability and performance than state-of-the-art baselines, validating the feasibility and effectiveness of TCCO for wireless networks.

  <summary>Details</summary>

We propose a body-scale NFC networking system that extends NFC coverage around the body, enabling surface-to-multipoint communication with distributed NFC sensor tags. This demonstration introduces two key technologies: Meander NFC and picoRing NFC. First, Meander NFC expands a clothing-based NFC networking area up to body scale while enabling a stable readout of small NFC tags occupying 1% of the coverage area. Meander NFC uses a meander coil which creates a spatially confined inductive field along the textile surface, ensuring robust coupling with small tags while preventing undesired electromagnetic body coupling. Second, picoRing NFC solves the weak inductive coupling caused by distance and size mismatches. By leveraging middle-range NFC and coil optimization, picoRing NFC extends the communication range to connect these disparate nodes between the ring and wristband.

Method: 1. 设计了一种真实性保障的拍卖机制来解决SP间的部署竞争；2. 进行了博弈论分析以证明资源分配问题的可解性；3. 开发了一种具有强容错能力的弹性联邦强化学习(FRL)解决方案，以应对传输错误和恶意竞争，同时促进自利SP间的潜在合作。

Abstract: The low-altitude economy (LAE) is a rapidly emerging paradigm that builds a service-centric economic ecosystem through large-scale and sustainable uncrewed aerial vehicle (UAV)-enabled service provisioning, reflecting the transition of the 6G era from technological advancement toward commercial deployment. In this paper, we study a realistic LAE scenario in which multiple SPs dynamically deploy UAVs to deliver multiple services to user hotspots, aiming to jointly optimize communication and computation resource allocation. To resolve deployment competition among SPs, an authenticity-guaranteed auction mechanism is designed, and game-theoretic analysis is conducted to establish the solvability of the proposed resource allocation problem. Furthermore, a resilient federated reinforcement learning (FRL)-based solution is developed with strong fault tolerance, effectively countering transmission errors and malicious competition while facilitating potential cooperation among self-interested SPs. Simulation results demonstrate that the proposed approach significantly improves service performance and robustness compared with baseline methods, providing a practical and scalable solution for competitive LAE service deployment.

### [15] [Adaptive Personalized Federated Reinforcement Learning for RIS-Assisted Aerial Relays in SAGINs with Fluid Antennas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04788)
*Yuxuan Yang,Bin Lyu,Abbas Jamalipour*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文研究了一种由低轨卫星星座通过RIS辅助的无人机中继，为配备FAS和传统天线的地面热点用户服务的空天地一体化网络（SAGIN）。针对环境动态性和异构性带来的挑战，提出了一种基于分层Stackelberg博弈的多热点下行速率最大化问题，并设计了自适应个性化联邦强化学习（FRL）算法来联合优化无人机轨迹和RIS相位控制。仿真表明该方法在动态异构场景下性能优越。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 空天地一体化网络（SAGIN）集成了卫星、无人机和地面设备，并结合了可重构智能表面（RIS）和流体天线系统（FAS），显著提升了无线环境的可控性。然而，跨层设施与无线电增强技术的紧密集成导致了显著的环境动态性和异构性，给大规模SAGIN的系统建模和优化带来了根本性挑战。因此，需要一种能够适应这种复杂动态环境的高效优化方法。

Method: 1. 建立系统模型：明确捕捉卫星移动性、无人机轨迹、RIS相位控制以及异构用户接收能力。
2. 问题建模：构建多热点下行链路速率最大化问题，并通过分层Stackelberg博弈分析其可解性。
3. 算法设计：提出一种自适应个性化联邦强化学习（FRL）算法，用于在异质且时变的多热点环境中自适应地优化无人机轨迹和RIS相位控制。

Result: 仿真结果显示，所提出的自适应个性化联邦强化学习算法在多热点下行链路速率方面表现出优越的性能。结果验证了该算法中“个性化”机制在动态异构SAGIN场景中的有效性，能够有效应对环境的不确定性和异构性。

Conclusion: 通过将RIS和FAS技术融入SAGIN架构，并利用分层Stackelberg博弈和自适应个性化联邦强化学习算法，可以有效解决因环境动态性和异构性导致的系统优化难题。该方法不仅提升了多热点场景下的下行链路速率，还证明了个性化联邦学习在应对复杂无线网络环境方面的巨大潜力。

Abstract: Space-air-ground integrated networks (SAGINs) interconnect satellites, uncrewed aerial vehicles (UAVs), and ground devices to enable flexible and ubiquitous wireless services. The integration of reconfigurable intelligent surfaces (RISs) and fluid antenna systems (FASs) further enhances radio environment controllability. However, the tight integration of cross-layer facilities and radio enhancement technologies leads to pronounced environmental dynamics and heterogeneity, posing fundamental challenges for system modeling and optimization in large-scale SAGINs. This paper investigates a SAGIN in which low Earth orbit (LEO) satellite constellations communicate with multiple ground hotspots via RIS-assisted UAV relays, serving both FAS-equipped and conventional users. A system model is developed that explicitly captures satellite mobility, UAV trajectories, RIS phase control, and heterogeneous user reception capabilities. Accordingly, a multi-hotspot downlink rate maximization problem is studied, whose solvability is analyzed through a hierarchical Stackelberg game. To address heterogeneous and time-varying multi-hotspot environments, an adaptive personalized federated reinforcement learning (FRL) algorithm is proposed for adaptive optimization of UAV trajectories and RIS phase controls. Simulation results demonstrate superior performance and validate the effectiveness of personalization in dynamic heterogeneous SAGIN scenarios.

</details>


### [16] [Analysis of Proactive Uncoordinated Techniques to Mitigate Interference in FMCW Automotive Radars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04944)
*Alessandro Bazzi,Francesco Miccoli,Fabrizio Cuccoli,Luca Facheris,Vincent Martinez*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 研究评估了多车FMCW雷达在密集场景下的互扰风险，并比较了三种无需车辆间协调的抗干扰方法。结果表明，基于啁啾（chirp-by-chirp）的频率跳变结合大带宽最有效，而基于指南针的方法性价比低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着现代车辆广泛采用毫米波雷达作为ADAS核心传感器，同频段内雷达数量激增导致严重的相互干扰问题，可能引发系统故障和安全隐患。现有研究缺乏对全FMCW雷达场景下干扰概率及不同无协作抗干扰策略的系统性评估。

Method: 构建了考虑相关干扰和主要雷达参数设置的新型模型，模拟真实的道路交通场景。研究对比了三种主动抗干扰技术：(1) 帧级随机载波频率跳变；(2) 啁啾级随机载波频率跳变；(3) 针对反向干扰的方向性指南针法（可与其他方法组合）。评估指标为雷达功能失效的概率。

Result: 密集交通场景下雷达失效风险显著。在所有测试方法中，啁啾级频率跳变（Chirp-by-chirp frequency hopping）在配合足够大的带宽时表现最佳，能最有效地降低干扰并保障系统可靠性。相比之下，基于指南针的方向性方法效果有限，其带来的额外系统复杂度不值得投入。

Conclusion: 在无需车辆间通信的约束下，实施啁啾级随机频率跳变是应对高密度FMCW雷达互扰的最优工程方案，但必须确保足够的信号带宽；而方向性辅助手段在实际应用中收益较低。

Abstract: Modern vehicles increasingly rely on advanced driver-assistance systems (ADAS), with radars playing a key role due to their cost-effectiveness and reliable performance. However, the growing number of radars operating in the same spectrum raises concerns about mutual interference, which could lead to system malfunctions and potential safety risks. This study focuses on a scenario in which all vehicles are equipped with frequency-modulated continuous-wave (FMCW) radars, and it assesses the impact of interference on radar functionality - expressed in terms of probability of failure - by considering both direct and reflected signals. The radars may employ one of the following proactive mitigation methods to reduce the impact of interference, all of which require no inter-vehicle coordination but differ in complexity: (i) random carrier-frequency hopping on a frame-by-frame basis, (ii) random carrier-frequency hopping on a chirp-by-chirp basis, and (iii) a directional, compass-based method specifically addressing interference from opposite directions, which can be combined with either of the two previous methods. In this work, we assume realistic simulated road traffic scenarios and develop a novel model that captures correlated interference and accounts for the main radar setting parameters. Results reveal that dense scenarios pose a high risk of radar malfunctions. Among the analyzed methods, chirp-by-chirp frequency hopping emerges as the most effective approach to mitigate interference and ensure system reliability, but only when combined with a sufficiently large bandwidth. The compass-based method, on the other hand, shows limited effectiveness and appears not worth the additional system complexity.

Moveover delegates trajectory and speed profile selection to individual vehicles, allowing each CAV to optimize them according to its unique kinematic characteristics. The algorithm is rigorously evaluated under both ideal and non-ideal networking conditions, specifically modeling 4G and 5G communication delays, across multiple layouts including single-lane, multi-lane, and roundabouts. ### [18] [AMV-L: Lifecycle-Managed Agent Memory for Tail-Latency Control in Long-Running LLM Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04443)
*Emmanuel Bamidele*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: Summary generation failed


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Motivation analysis unavailable

Method: Method extraction failed

Result: Result analysis unavailable

Conclusion: Conclusion extraction failed

Abstract: Long-running LLM agents require persistent memory to preserve state across interactions, yet most deployed systems manage memory with age-based retention (e.g., TTL). While TTL bounds item lifetime, it does not bound the computational footprint of memory on the request path: as retained items accumulate, retrieval candidate sets and vector similarity scans can grow unpredictably, yielding heavy-tailed latency and unstable throughput. We present AMV-L (Adaptive Memory Value Lifecycle), a memory-management framework that treats agent memory as a managed systems resource. AMV-L assigns each memory item a continuously updated utility score and uses value-driven promotion, demotion, and eviction to maintain lifecycle tiers; retrieval is restricted to a bounded, tier-aware candidate set that decouples the request-path working set from total retained memory. We implement AMV-L in a full-stack LLM serving system and evaluate it under identical long-running workloads against two baselines: TTL and an LRU working-set policy, with fixed prompt-injection caps. Relative to TTL, AMV-L improves throughput by 3.1x and reduces latency by 4.2x (median), 4.7x (p95), and 4.4x (p99), while reducing the fraction of requests exceeding 2s from 13.8% to 0.007%. Compared to LRU, AMV-L trades a small regression in median/p95 latency (+26% / +3%) for improved extreme-tail behavior (-15% p99; -98% >2s) and lower token overhead (approximately 6% fewer tokens/request), while matching retrieval quality (value means within approximately 0-2%). The gains arise primarily from bounding retrieval-set size and vector-search work, not from shortening prompts. Our results show that predictable performance for long-running LLM agents requires explicit control of memory working-set size and value-driven lifecycle management, rather than retention time alone.

</details>


### [19] [Overcoming Latency-bound Limitations of Distributed Graph Algorithms using the HPX Runtime System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04583)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有分布式图处理框架（如Spark GraphX和PBGL）在处理图的不规则结构时面临负载不均衡、同步开销大及延迟敏感等挑战，难以高效支持大规模图计算。

Method: 基于C++的NWgraph机制与HPX运行时，利用其分布式容器和异步构造，构建统一执行模型；该模型在本地共享内存内利用并行性，跨局部性重叠通信与计算，并透明管理异步操作。

Result: 实验表明，HPX实现的三种算法（遍历、中心性、模式匹配）在性能上显著优于GraphX和PBGL，主要得益于异步执行、延迟隐藏及细粒度并行性的有效利用。

Abstract: Graph processing at scale presents many challenges, including the irregular structure of graphs, the latency-bound nature of graph algorithms, and the overhead associated with distributed execution. While existing frameworks such as Spark GraphX and the Parallel Boost Graph Library (PBGL) have introduced abstractions for distributed graph processing, they continue to struggle with inherent issues like load imbalance and synchronization overhead. In this work, we present a distributed library prototype and a distributed implementation of three key graph algorithms - Breadth-First Search (BFS), PageRank, and Triangle Counting, using C++ mechanisms from the NWgraph library and leveraging HPX's distributed containers and asynchronous constructs. These algorithms span the categories of Traversal, centrality, and Pattern matching, and are selected to represent diverse computational characteristics. We evaluate our HPX-based implementations against GraphX, and PBGL, showing that a high-performance runtime such as HPX enables the construction of algorithms that significantly outperform conventional frameworks by exploiting asynchronous execution, latency hiding, and fine-grained parallelism in shared memory. All algorithms in our prototype follow a unified execution model in which local and remote computations are expressed using the same programming abstractions, with asynchrony managed transparently by the runtime. This design explicitly leverages shared-memory parallelism within each locality while overlapping communication and computation across localities, providing a practical foundation for extending this approach to a broader class of distributed graph algorithms.

### [20] [DuaLip-GPU Technical Report](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04621)
*Gregory Dexter,Aida Rahmattalabi,Sanjana Garg,Qinquan Song,Ruby Tu,Yuan Gao,Yi Zhang,Zhipeng Wang,Rahul Mazumder*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 提出一种解耦问题规范与优化引擎、面向GPU执行的大规模线性规划求解器，通过算子中心模型和稀疏匹配约束的专用技术，在极端规模匹配任务上实现10倍加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大规模线性规划求解器（如ECLIPSE和DuaLip）虽能扩展，但紧耦合于少量模式且基于CPU-centric的Scala/Spark栈，限制了可扩展性并无法有效利用现代加速器。

Method: 采用算子中心编程模型，将LP公式表达为可组合原语；开发针对稀疏匹配约束的GPU执行技术（包括约束对齐稀疏布局、批处理投影核及仅通信对偶变量的分布式设计）；改进岭正则化对偶上升法，引入Jacobi风格行归一化、原始缩放及正则参数延续方案。

Result: 在极端规模匹配工作负载下，GPU实现在保持收敛保证的前提下，相比之前分布式CPU DuaLip求解器实现了至少10倍的墙钟时间加速。

Conclusion: 通过架构解耦和GPU专用优化技术，该求解器成功解决了大规模线性规划的可扩展性和加速问题，为重复性决策系统提供了高效解决方案。

Abstract: Large-scale linear programs (LPs) arise in many decision systems, including ranking, allocation, and matching problems that must be solved repeatedly at massive scale. Prior work such as ECLIPSE and LinkedIn's open-source DuaLip showed that ridge-regularized dual ascent with first-order methods can scale to these settings. However, the original implementation was tightly coupled to a small number of schemas and built on a CPU-centric Scala/Spark stack, limiting extensibility and preventing effective use of modern accelerators.
  We present a redesigned solver architecture that decouples problem specification from the optimization engine and targets GPU execution. The system uses an operator-centric programming model in which LP formulations are expressed through composable primitives for dual objective evaluation and blockwise projection operators for decomposable constraint families. This design allows new formulations to be added locally while reusing a shared optimization loop, diagnostics, and distributed infrastructure.
  To realize the available parallelism, we develop GPU execution techniques tailored to sparse matching constraints, including constraint-aligned sparse layouts, batched projection kernels, and a distributed design that communicates only dual variables. Further, we improve the underlying ridge-regularized dual ascent method with Jacobi-style row normalization, primal scaling, and a continuation scheme for the regularization parameter.
  On extreme-scale matching workloads, the GPU implementation achieves at least a 10x wall-clock speedup over the prior distributed CPU DuaLip solver under matched stopping criteria, while maintaining convergence guarantees.

### [21] [SLO-Aware Compute Resource Allocation for Prefill-Decode Disaggregated LLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04716)
*Luchang Li,Dongfang Li,Bozhao Gong,Yu Zhang*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合理论建模与实证基准测试的混合方法，用于在满足吞吐量、SLO及请求特征（输入/输出长度）约束下，确定大语言模型推理中预填充-解码（P/D）分离架构的最佳硬件资源分配方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管P/D分离已成为LLM推理的主流优化策略，但目前缺乏一套成熟的方法论，能够在总吞吐量、服务等级目标（SLOs）以及具体请求特征（如输入和输出长度）的约束下，确定最优的P/D硬件资源配置数量。

Method: 1. 构建理论模型：基于总吞吐量需求、请求的输入/输出长度以及预填充和解码阶段的吞吐量来计算P/D资源数量。
2. 预填充阶段建模：利用M/M/1排队论对预填充过程进行建模，结合基准测试的最大预填充吞吐量和首字延迟（TTFT），推导满足SLO约束下的实际预填充吞吐量。
3. 解码阶段测量：通过实证测量确定满足每输出令牌时间（TPOT）要求的解码批次大小，并据此计算对应的解码吞吐量。
4. 混合验证：将理论计算与实证基准测试相结合，以预测最佳资源分配。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法能够准确预测现实世界LLM推理场景中的最佳P/D资源分配，有效解决了在复杂约束条件下资源规划的问题。

Conclusion: 该研究填补了P/D资源规划领域的空白，提供了一种可量化且经过验证的方法，帮助系统在满足严格SLO和吞吐量要求的同时，实现硬件资源的最优配置。

Abstract: Prefill-Decode (P/D) disaggregation has emerged as a widely adopted optimization strategy for Large Language Model (LLM) inference. However, there currently exists no well-established methodology for determining the optimal number of P/D hardware resources, subject to constraints on total throughput, service level objectives (SLOs), and request characteristics - specifically input and output lengths. To address this gap, we propose a hybrid approach that combines theoretical modeling with empirical benchmarking. First, we present a theoretical model for calculating P/D resource counts, which is based on total throughput requirements, request input and output lengths, as well as prefill and decode throughput. Then, to obtain the actual prefill and decode throughput under SLO constraints, we model the prefill process using M/M/1 queuing theory, deriving the achieved prefill throughput from the benchmarked maximum prefill throughput and Time-To-First-Token (TTFT). For the decode phase, we determine the decode batch sizes that meet Time-Per-Output-Token (TPOT) requirements and obtain the corresponding decode throughput through empirical measurements. Our experimental results demonstrate that the proposed method can accurately predict optimal P/D resource allocation in real-world LLM inference scenarios.

</details>


### [22] [The Semantic Arrow of Time, Part III: RDMA and the Completion Fallacy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04774)
*Paul Borrill*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文指出RDMA技术的完成语义存在“完成谬误”（completion fallacy），即仅保证数据写入远程网卡缓冲区，而未确保被接收端应用语义整合。通过分析Meta、Google、Microsoft等工业级案例，揭示了信号完成与应用语义满足之间的巨大时间差，并论证唯有包含强制反射阶段的协议架构才能彻底解决此问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前两部分论文已提出计算领域的“语义时间箭头”及OAE链接状态机模型。本文旨在探讨当这些原则在工业规模下被违反时会发生什么，特别是针对当前高性能数据传输技术RDMA中存在的潜在缺陷及其对大规模集群的影响。

Method: 1. 理论分析：揭示RDMA完成语义中的类别错误，定义“完成谬误”。2. 过程追踪：通过RDMA Write操作的七个时间阶段，量化完成信号与语义满足之间的差距。3. 实证研究：深入分析四个工业界案例（Meta的RoCE网络、Google的1RMA重构、Microsoft的DCQCN故障、SDR-RDMA部分完成）。4. 对比评估：比较CXL 3.0、NVLink和UALink等技术方案的有效性。

Result: 研究表明，RDMA的完成信号与应用程序的语义满足之间可能存在任意大的时间差。现有的替代技术（如CXL 3.0、NVLink、UALink）虽能缓解部分问题，但均无法根除该谬误。所有案例分析均证实了缺乏强制反射阶段会导致数据一致性与语义完整性风险。

Conclusion: 要消除交付与承诺之间的差距，必须采用包含强制反射阶段（mandatory reflecting phase）的协议架构。这是解决工业级高性能数据传输中语义不完整问题的唯一根本途径。

Abstract: This is the third of five papers comprising The Semantic Arrow of Time. Parts I and II identified computing's hidden semantic arrow of time, the FITO category mistake, and presented the constructive alternative: the OAE link state machine with its mandatory reflecting phase.
  This paper examines what happens when those principles are violated at industrial scale. Remote Direct Memory Access (RDMA) is the highest-performance data movement technology in production, deployed across Meta's 24,000-GPU clusters, Google's data centers, and Microsoft's Azure infrastructure. We argue that RDMA's completion semantics contain a category mistake: they guarantee placement (data written to a remote NIC buffer) but not commitment (data semantically integrated by the receiving application). We call this the completion fallacy.
  We document the fallacy through seven temporal stages of an RDMA Write operation, showing that the gap between completion signal and application semantic satisfaction can be arbitrarily large. We trace consequences through four case studies: Meta's RoCE fabric, Google's 1RMA redesign, Microsoft's DCQCN failures, and SDR-RDMA partial completions.
  A comparative analysis shows CXL 3.0, NVLink, and UALink each address parts of the completion fallacy but none eliminates it entirely. Only a protocol architecture with a mandatory reflecting phase can close the gap between delivery and commitment.

</details>


### [23] [Unlocking Python's Cores: Hardware Usage and Energy Implications of Removing the GIL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04782)
*José Daniel Montoya Salazar*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: Python 3.14.2的无GIL构建在并行izable工作负载上显著提升了执行速度和能效，但增加了内存开销；而顺序或高锁竞争的工作负载则性能下降且能耗增加。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管Python 3.13起允许实验性禁用全局解释器锁（GIL）以提升多核并行能力，但此前研究多关注速度提升，对能耗、硬件利用率及内存影响的研究不足。本研究旨在填补这一空白，全面评估无GIL模式下的综合性能表现。

Method: 通过对比Python 3.14.2的GIL启用与禁用版本，在四类工作负载（NumPy基础、顺序内核、线程化数值计算、线程化对象操作）下，测量并分析执行时间、CPU利用率、内存使用量及能耗数据。

Result: 对于独立数据的并行工作负载，无GIL版本可将执行时间缩短至原来的1/4，能耗同步降低，CPU多核利用率显著提升，但内存占用增加；顺序工作负载能耗反而增加13-43%；高频共享对象修改导致性能退化。总体显示能耗与执行时间成正比，无GIL并未改变功率特性，但内存（尤其是虚拟内存）普遍上升，归因于对象级锁机制、运行时线程安全增强及新内存分配器的引入。

Conclusion: Python的无GIL构建并非通用优化方案。开发者在采用前需评估其工作负载是否具备有效并行执行的能力，以避免在顺序或高锁竞争场景下遭受性能与能耗的双重损失。

Abstract: Python's Global Interpreter Lock prevents execution on more than one CPU core at the same time, even when multiple threads are used. However, starting with Python 3.13 an experimental build allows disabling the GIL. While prior work has examined speedup implications of this disabling, the effects on energy consumption and hardware utilization have received less attention. This study measures execution time, CPU utilization, memory usage, and energy consumption using four workload categories: NumPy-based, sequential kernels, threaded numerical workloads, and threaded object workloads, comparing GIL and free-threaded builds of Python 3.14.2.
  The results highlight a trade-off. For parallelizable workloads operating on independent data, the free-threaded build reduces execution time by up to 4 times, with a proportional reduction in energy consumption, and effective multi-core utilization, at the cost of an increase in memory usage. In contrast, sequential workloads do not benefit from removing the GIL and instead show a 13-43% increase in energy consumption. Similarly, workloads where threads frequently access and modify the same objects show reduced improvements or even degradation due to lock contention. Across all workloads, energy consumption is proportional to execution time, indicating that disabling the GIL does not significantly affect power consumption, even when CPU utilization increases. When it comes to memory, the no-GIL build shows a general increase, more visible in virtual memory than in physical memory. This increase is primarily attributed to per-object locking, additional thread-safety mechanisms in the runtime, and the adoption of a new memory allocator.
  These findings suggest that Python's no-GIL build is not a universal improvement. Developers should evaluate whether their workload can effectively benefit from parallel execution before adoption.

</details>


### [24] [The Semantic Arrow of Time, Part IV: Why Transactions Fail](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04810)
*Paul Borrill*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文是《语义时间之箭》系列的第四篇，指出“仅向前”的时间假设（FITO范畴错误）在文件同步、电子邮件和记忆系统中导致语义破坏，揭示了缺乏反射机制的系统无法区分成功集成与单纯的时间顺序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在将前文提出的FITO范畴错误从数据中心扩展到日常系统，分析那些因依赖单向时间流而丧失语义完整性的领域，揭示其背后的共同结构模式。

Method: 通过考察三个具体领域（文件同步、电子邮件、记忆），识别出所有系统中普遍存在的结构性模式：在没有反射阶段的情况下提交状态变更，从而无法验证语义完整性。

Result: 研究发现，云平台的“最后写入者获胜”策略导致内容丢失，基于时间戳的邮件排序产生幽灵消息和因果违规，以及人和人工智能的记忆重构过程因缺乏事务保障而产生系统性语义腐败；这些现象均源于FITO范畴错误在不同尺度上的运作。

Conclusion: 只要系统将信息的向前流动视为意义的充分证据，语义时间之箭就会被违反；第五篇将提出“莱布尼茨桥”作为统一框架，以在所有五个领域中填补这一语义鸿沟。

Abstract: This is the fourth of five papers comprising The Semantic Arrow of Time. Parts I-III established that computing's hidden arrow of time is semantic rather than thermodynamic, that bilateral transaction protocols create causal order through a mandatory reflecting phase, and that RDMA's completion semantics implement the FITO category mistake at industrial scale.
  This paper traces the consequences of the FITO category mistake beyond the data center, into systems people use every day. We examine three domains where forward-only temporal assumptions destroy meaning: file synchronization, where cloud platforms silently delete user content because last-writer-wins cannot represent distributed causality; email, where timestamp-based ordering produces phantom messages, causality violations, and stuck synchronization; and memory--both human and artificial--where reconstructive processes that operate without transactional guarantees produce systematic semantic corruption.
  In each domain, we identify the same structural pattern: a system that commits state changes forward in time without a reflecting phase, and that therefore cannot distinguish between successful semantic integration and mere temporal succession. The pattern is not coincidental. It is the FITO category mistake operating at different scales: bytes in a NIC buffer, files in a cloud, messages in an inbox, engrams in a hippocampus, tokens in a transformer.
  We conclude that the semantic arrow of time is violated whenever a system treats the forward flow of information as sufficient evidence of meaning. Part V will show how the Leibniz Bridge provides a unified framework for closing this gap across all five domains.

### [25] [The Semantic Arrow of Time, Part V: The Leibniz Bridge -- Toward a Unified Theory of Semantic Time](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04826)
*Paul Borrill*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文是“语义时间之箭”系列五篇论文的终章，构建了“莱布尼茨桥”统一框架，将哲学基础（莱布尼茨的不可分辨者同一性）、协议工程（OAE的双边交易结构）与物理底层（量子力学中的不定因果序）相连接。核心原则是互信息守恒，指出时间方向源于可逆交换在熵产生时的承诺，而非公理。该框架将FLP、两将军和CAP定理重新解释为FITO系统的定理而非物理限制，并提出了三角形网络作为无需集中协调的最小语义一致性拓扑。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 证明了互信息守恒原则能够消解FLP、两将军问题和CAP定理所宣称的“不可能性”，揭示这些定理实际上是针对FITO系统而非物理本质的限制。研究确立了三角形网络为在无中心协调下实现语义一致性的最小拓扑结构。此外，该框架成功将哲学本体论、协议工程设计与物理底层机制统一在一个连贯的理论体系中。

Conclusion: 当放弃FITO假设时，分布式计算的形态将发生根本性转变。本文提出的“莱布尼茨桥”不仅解决了长期存在的分布式一致性悖论，还为理解时间箭头提供了新的视角：时间并非先验公理，而是可逆交换在信息守恒约束下发生熵产生的结果。未来工作需进一步探索基于此新范式的分布式系统设计及其对语义一致性的深层影响。

Abstract: This is the final paper in the five-part series The Semantic Arrow of Time. Part I identified the FITO category mistake -- treating forward temporal flow as sufficient for establishing meaning. Part II presented the constructive alternative: the OAE link state machine with its mandatory reflecting phase. Part III showed the FITO fallacy operating at industrial scale in RDMA completion semantics. Part IV traced the same pattern through file synchronization, email, human memory, and language model hallucination.
  This paper closes the series by constructing the Leibniz Bridge: a unified framework that connects the philosophical foundations (Leibniz's Identity of Indiscernibles, as formalized by Spekkens), the protocol engineering (OAE's bilateral transaction structure), and the physical substrate (indefinite causal order in quantum mechanics). The bridge rests on a single principle: mutual information conservation -- the requirement that every causal exchange preserve the total information accessible to both endpoints, with the direction of time emerging not from axiom but from entropy production when a reversible exchange commits.
  We show that this principle dissolves the apparent impossibility of the FLP, Two Generals, and CAP theorems by revealing them as theorems about FITO systems, not about physics. We present the triangle network as the minimal topology for semantic consistency without centralized coordination. We conclude with open questions and a reflection on what distributed computing looks like when the FITO assumption is dropped.

Abstract: We study the classical Election problem in anonymous net- works, where solutions can rely on the use of random bits, which may be either shared or unshared among nodes. We provide a complete char- acterization of the conditions under which a randomized Election algo- rithm exists, for arbitrary structural knowledge. Our analysis considers both Las Vegas and Monte Carlo randomized algorithms, under the as- sumptions of shared and unshared randomness. In our setting, random sources are considered shared if the output bits are identical across spe- cific subsets of nodes. The algorithms and impossibility proofs are extensions of those of [5] for the deterministic setting. Our results are a complete generalization of those from [8]. Moreover, as applications, we consider many specific knowledge: no knowledge, a bound on the size, a bound on the number of nodes sharing a source, the size, or the full topology of the network. For each of them, we show how the general characterizations apply, showing they actually correspond to classes of structural knowledge. We also de- scribe also how randomized Election algorithms from the literature fits in this landscape. We therefore provide a comprehensive picture illustrating how knowledge influences the computability of the Election problem in arbitrary anonymous graphs with shared randomness.

### [30] [Radiation Hydrodynamics at Scale: Comparing MPI and Asynchronous Many-Task Runtimes with FleCSI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05366)
*Alexander Strack,Hartmut Kaiser,Dirk Pflüger*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文评估了FleCSI框架在MPI、Legion和HPX三种后端上的性能，通过Poisson求解器和HARD辐射流体动力学代码的基准测试，发现HPX后端在计算密集型任务上优于MPI+Kokkos，而Legion存在显著开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分布式代码编写复杂且耗时，FleCSI旨在提供高层编程接口简化开发，但需量化其引入的不同运行时后端（特别是AMTR）的性能优势与开销。

Method: 选取简单的Poisson求解器（通信密集）和HARD辐射流体动力学代码（计算密集）作为应用，在最高1024个节点上对FleCSI的MPI、Legion和HPX三个后端进行基准测试，分析弱缩放和强缩放下的并行效率及性能差距。

Result: 在Poisson求解器中，MPI后端实现超过97%的并行效率，Legion开销大且扩展性受限，HPX仅引入边际开销但受限于非优化的集体操作；在HARD计算密集型基准中，HPX在少于64个节点时优于MPI+Kokkos（弱缩加速比1.31，强缩1.27），在纯流体动力学部分于少于32节点时分别比MPI和MPI+Kokcos快1.20倍和1.64倍。

Conclusion: FleCSI的抽象层在通信密集型任务中开销极小，HPX后端在计算密集型应用中展现出优于MPI+Kokkos的性能潜力，但其可扩展性目前受限于HPX集体操作的优化程度，而Legion后端在当前实现下存在明显性能瓶颈。

Abstract: Writing efficient distributed code remains a labor-intensive and complex endeavor. To simplify application development, the Flexible Computational Science Infrastructure (FleCSI) framework offers a user-oriented, high-level programming interface that is built upon a task-based runtime model. Internally, FleCSI integrates state-of-the-art parallelization backends, including MPI and the asynchronous many-task runtimes (AMTRs) Legion and HPX, enabling applications to fully leverage asynchronous parallelism. In this work, we benchmark two applications using FleCSI's three backends on up to 1024 nodes, intending to quantify the advantages and overheads introduced by the AMTR backends. As representative applications, we select a simple Poisson solver and the multidimensional radiation hydrodynamics code HARD. In the communication-focused Poisson solver benchmark, FleCSI achieves over 97% parallel efficiency using the MPI backend under weak scaling on up to 131072 cores, indicating that only minimal overhead is introduced by its abstraction layer. While the Legion backend exhibits notable overheads and scaling limitations, the HPX backend introduces only marginal overhead compared to MPI+Kokkos. However, the scalability of the HPX backend is currently limited due to the usage of non-optimized HPX collective operations. In the computation-focused radiation hydrodynamics benchmarks, the performance gap between the MPI and HPX backends fades. On fewer than 64 nodes, the HPX backend outperforms MPI+Kokkos, achieving an average speedup of 1.31 under weak scaling and up to 1.27 under strong scaling. For the hydrodynamics-only HARD benchmark, the HPX backend demonstrates superior performance on fewer than 32 nodes, achieving speedups of up to 1.20 relative to MPI and up to 1.64 relative to MPI+Kokkos.

</details>

### [31] [HDLFORGE: A Two-Stage Multi-Agent Framework for Efficient Verilog Code Generation with Adaptive Model Escalation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04646)
*Armin Abdollahi,Saeid Shokoufa,Negin Ashrafi,Mehdi Kamal,Massoud Pedram*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: HDLFORGE 是一个两阶段多智能体框架，用于自动生成 Verilog 代码。它默认使用中等规模 LLM 进行快速生成，仅在必要时通过校准评分升级到超大规模 LLM，从而在生成速度和准确性之间取得最佳平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的单一阶段系统难以同时兼顾 Verilog 代码生成的速度与准确性。需要在保证高准确率的同时，显著降低生成延迟和计算成本，特别是在处理复杂硬件描述语言任务时。

Method: 提出了一种两阶段架构：Stage A 使用紧凑型编码器和中等规模 LLM；Stage B 仅在诊断测试（编译、lint、烟雾测试）的校准分数表明需要时，才调用强编码器和超大规模 LLM。核心创新包括一个反例引导的形式化智能体，将有限模型检测轨迹转换为可复用的微测试，以加速错误检测和修复；以及一个可移植的升级控制器，无需修改现有 Verilog LLM 管道即可集成。

Result: 在 VerilogEval Human、VerilogEval V2 和 RTLLM 基准测试中，HDLFORGE-Qwen 表现优异：在 VerilogEval Human 上 Pass@1 达到 91.2%，在 VerilogEval V2 上达到 91.8%，且中位延迟比单阶段系统降低了约 50%；在 RTLLM 上 Pass@5 达到 97.2%。分析显示其在准确性与延迟的权衡上优于单阶段系统。

Conclusion: HDLFORGE 通过动态资源分配和形式化验证辅助，成功实现了 Verilog 生成速度与准确性的双重优化，为自动化硬件设计提供了高效且可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: We present HDLFORGE, a two-stage multi-agent framework for automated Verilog generation that optimizes the trade-off between generation speed and accuracy. The system uses a compact coder with a medium-sized LLM by default (Stage A) and escalates to a stronger coder with an ultra-large LLM (Stage B) only when needed, guided by a calibrated score from inexpensive diagnostics including compilation, lint, and smoke tests. A key innovation is a counterexample-guided formal agent that converts bounded-model-checking traces into reusable micro-tests, significantly reducing bug detection time and repair iterations. The portable escalation controller can wrap existing Verilog LLM pipelines without modifying their internals. Evaluated on VerilogEval Human, VerilogEval V2, and RTLLM benchmarks, HDLFORGE demonstrates improved accuracy-latency trade-offs compared to single-stage systems through comprehensive analysis of wall-clock time distributions, escalation thresholds, and agent ablations. On VerilogEval Human and VerilogEval V2, HDLFORGE-Qwen achieves 91.2% and 91.8% Pass@1 with roughly 50% lower median latency, dramatically improving accuracy over other medium-sized models, and 97.2% Pass@5 on RTLLM.

</details>


### [32] [Hardware-Software Co-design for 3D-DRAM-based LLM Serving Accelerator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04797)
*Cong Li,Yihan Yin,Chenhao Xue,Zhao Wang,Fujun Bai,Yixin Guo,Xiping Jiang,Qiang Wu,Yuan Xie,Guangyu Sun*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: Helios是一款基于混合绑定的LLM服务加速器，旨在解决现有近存处理（NMP）设计在应对动态LLM工作负载时存在的KV缓存管理粗糙和注意力执行流程僵化问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的NMP设计采用粗粒度的KV缓存管理和不灵活的注意力执行流，无法有效处理具有高度动态性的LLM服务工作负载（如请求到达率波动和长度变化），从而限制了其加速LLM服务的能力。

Method: 提出了一种混合绑定（Hybrid-bonding-based）架构：1. 设计了片内（intra-PE）执行流程和片间（inter-PE）通信原语，以支持分布式分块注意力执行；2. 提出了空间感知（spatially-aware）的KV缓存分配机制，以平衡注意力工作负载分布并最小化片间数据传输开销。

Result: 与现有的GPU/NMP设计相比，Helios实现了3.25倍（几何平均值）的速度提升和3.36倍（几何平均值）的能效提升，同时将令牌间延迟（time-between-tokens）降低了72%（P50）和76%（P99）。

Conclusion: Helios通过弥合LLM服务中动态KV缓存管理与NMP处理引擎之间非均匀内存抽象之间的差距，显著提升了LLM服务的性能和能效，为高效处理动态工作负载提供了新的解决方案。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have been widely deployed for online generative services, where numerous LLM instances jointly handle workloads with fluctuating request arrival rates and variable request lengths. To efficiently execute coexisting compute-intensive and memory-intensive operators, near-memory processing (NMP) based computing paradigm has been extensively proposed. However, existing NMP designs adopt coarse-grained KV cache management and inflexible attention execution flow. Such limitations hinder these proposals from efficiently handling \textit{highly dynamic} LLM serving workloads, limiting their ability to accelerate LLM serving.
  To tackle these problems, we propose Helios, a Hybrid-bonding-based \uline{L}LM \uline{S}erving accelerator. Helios aims to bridge the fundamental gap between the dynamic nature of KV cache management in LLM serving and the distributed, non-uniform memory abstraction among NMP processing engines (PEs). To this end, we design both the intra-PE execution flow and the inter-PE communication primitives for distributed tiled attention execution. We further propose \textit{spatially-aware} KV cache allocation mechanism to balance the attention workload distribution while minimizing the inter-PE data transfer overhead. Compared with existing GPU/NMP designs, Helios achieves 3.25 times (geomean) speedup and 3.36 times (geomean) better energy efficiency, along with up to 72%/76% P50/P99 time-between-tokens degradation.

### [33] [VMXDOTP: A RISC-V Vector ISA Extension for Efficient Microscaling (MX) Format Acceleration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04979)
*Max Wipfli,Gamze İslamoğlu,Navaneeth Kunhi Purayil,Angelo Garofalo,Luca Benini*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 提出VMXDOTP，一种RISC-V向量ISA扩展指令，用于高效执行微缩放（MX）格式的点积运算，解决MX语义与向量执行不匹配导致的资源利用率低问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代基于解码器的Transformer模型需要灵活的加速器，而微缩放（MX）数据格式虽能减少数据量，但其块浮点（BFP）语义和多步混合精度操作破坏了向量流水线的规则性，导致计算资源利用不足和性能下降。

Method: 设计了一种名为VMXDOTP的RISC-V向量1.0 ISA扩展指令，支持MXFP8和MXFP4输入、FP32和BF16累加以及软件定义的块大小；将其集成到可扩展的高能效共享L1内存向量处理单元（VPE）集群中，并在12nm FinFET工艺下实现。

Result: VMXDOTP增强的VPE集群在MX-MatMul上达到97%的利用率；在1GHz、0.8V下实现高达125 MXFP8-GFLOPS和250 MXFP4-GFLOPS的吞吐量，能效达843/1632 GFLOPS/W；相比软件模拟方案，速度提升7.0倍，能效提升4.9倍；相比现有MX引擎，面积效率提升1.4倍，能效提升2.1倍，且仅增加7.2%的面积开销。

Conclusion: VMXDOTP通过硬件加速MX点积运算，有效解决了微缩放格式在向量架构上的执行瓶颈，显著提升了Transformer模型的推理效率和能效，为未来高带宽、大尺寸模型提供了高效的硬件解决方案。

Abstract: Compared to the first generation of deep neural networks, dominated by regular, compute-intensive kernels such as matrix multiplications (MatMuls) and convolutions, modern decoder-based transformers interleave attention, normalization, and data-dependent control flow. This demands flexible accelerators, a requirement met by scalable, highly energy-efficient shared-L1-memory vector processing element (VPE) clusters. Meanwhile, the ever-growing size and bandwidth needs of state-of-the-art models make reduced-precision formats increasingly attractive. Microscaling (MX) data formats, based on block floating-point (BFP) representations, have emerged as a promising solution to reduce data volumes while preserving accuracy. However, MX semantics are poorly aligned with vector execution: block scaling and multi-step mixed-precision operations break the regularity of vector pipelines, leading to underutilized compute resources and performance degradation. To address these challenges, we propose VMXDOTP, a RISC-V Vector (RVV) 1.0 instruction set architecture (ISA) extension for efficient MX dot product execution, supporting MXFP8 and MXFP4 inputs, FP32 and BF16 accumulation, and software-defined block sizes. A VMXDOTP-enhanced VPE cluster achieves up to 97 % utilization on MX-MatMul. Implemented in 12 nm FinFET, it achieves up to 125 MXFP8-GFLOPS and 250 MXFP4-GFLOPS, with 843/1632 MXFP8/MXFP4-GFLOPS/W at 1 GHz, 0.8 V, and only 7.2 % area overhead. Our design yields up to 7.0x speedup and 4.9x energy efficiency with respect to software-emulated MXFP8-MatMul. Compared with prior MX engines, VMXDOTP supports variable block sizes, is up to 1.4x more area-efficient, and delivers up to 2.1x higher energy efficiency.

</details>


### [34] [Network Design for Wafer-Scale Systems with Wafer-on-Wafer Hybrid Bonding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05266)
*Patrick Iff,Tommaso Bonato,Maciej Besta,Luca Benini,Torsten Hoefler*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文研究了晶圆级集成中光刻掩膜版（reticle）的物理布局对网络拓扑和通信性能的影响，提出四种改进布局方案，显著提升了吞吐量并降低了延迟和能耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着芯片间通信带宽急剧下降，基于Transformer的大语言模型受到数据移动的严重限制。晶圆级集成通过混合键合技术提供了极高的带内带宽，但掩膜版的物理布局方式尚未被充分研究其对网络性能和能效的影响。

Method: 以2D网格布局为基准，提出了四种新的掩膜版布局策略：对齐（Aligned）、交错（Interleaved）、旋转（Rotated）和轮廓（Contoured），并通过仿真分析这些布局对网络拓扑、吞吐量、延迟和能耗的影响。

Result: 相比基线布局，提出的四种新布局可将吞吐量提升高达250%，延迟降低高达36%，每字节传输能耗降低高达38%。

Conclusion: 在晶圆级集成的架构设计中，合理优化掩膜版的物理布局是提升通信性能、降低延迟和能耗的关键因素，为未来大规模AI硬件设计提供了重要指导。

Abstract: Transformer-based large language models are increasingly constrained by data movement as communication bandwidth drops sharply beyond the chip boundary. Wafer-scale integration using wafer-on-wafer hybrid bonding alleviates this limitation by providing ultra-high bandwidth between reticles on bonded wafers. In this paper, we investigate how the physical placement of reticles on wafers influences the achievable network topology and the resulting communication performance. Starting from a 2D mesh-like baseline, we propose four reticle placements (Aligned, Interleaved, Rotated, and Contoured) that improve throughput by up to 250%, reduce latency by up to 36%, and decrease energy per transmitted byte by up to 38%.

### [35] [NL2GDS: LLM-aided interface for Open Source Chip Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05489)
*Max Eland,Jeyan Thiyagalingam,Dinesh Pamunuwa,Roshan Weerasekera*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: NL2GDS 是一个利用大语言模型（LLMs）将自然语言硬件描述直接转换为可综合的 RTL 代码和完整 GDSII 布局的新框架，通过开源 OpenLane ASIC 流程实现自动化设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 硬件设计日益复杂，且高层规范与寄存器传输级（RTL）实现之间存在巨大差距，阻碍了快速原型设计和系统开发。

Method: 提出 NL2GDS 模块化流水线：捕捉非正式设计意图，利用多个 LLM 引擎生成 HDL 并进行验证，最后编排自动化综合与布局流程。

Result: 在 ISCAS'85 和 ISCAS'89 基准测试中，相比基线设计实现了高达 36% 的面积减少、35% 的延迟降低以及 70% 的功耗节省。

Abstract: The growing complexity of hardware design and the widening gap between high-level specifications and register-transfer level (RTL) implementation hinder rapid prototyping and system design. We introduce NL2GDS (Natural Language to Layout), a novel framework that leverages large language models (LLMs) to translate natural language hardware descriptions into synthesizable RTL and complete GDSII layouts via the open-source OpenLane ASIC flow. NL2GDS employs a modular pipeline that captures informal design intent, generates HDL using multiple LLM engines and verifies them, and orchestrates automated synthesis and layout. Evaluations on ISCAS'85 and ISCAS'89 benchmark designs demonstrate up to 36% area reduction, 35% delay reduction, and 70% power savings compared to baseline designs, highlighting its potential to democratize ASIC design and accelerate hardware innovation.

### [36] [GAIDE: Graph-based Attention Masking for Spatial- and Embodiment-aware Motion Planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04463)
*Davood Soleymanzadeh,Xiao Liang,Minghui Zheng*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于采样的运动规划算法在高维配置空间中面临样本效率低下的问题，而现有的神经启发式采样方法难以有效编码运动规划问题中固有的空间结构。

Method: 提出GAIDE方法，将规划问题的空间结构和机械臂的实体特征表示为图，并通过注意力掩码机制将其集成到基于Transformer的神经采样器中，从而指导采样分布的学习。

Result: 在均匀采样、手工启发式采样和现有神经启发式采样基准上的评估结果表明，GAIDE显著提高了规划效率和成功率。

Conclusion: 结合空间结构与实体特征的图注意力机制能有效解决高维空间中的样本效率问题，为机器人运动规划提供了更高效的解决方案。

Abstract: Sampling-based motion planning algorithms are widely used for motion planning of robotic manipulators, but they often struggle with sample inefficiency in high-dimensional configuration spaces due to their reliance on uniform or hand-crafted informed sampling primitives. Neural informed samplers address this limitation by learning the sampling distribution from prior planning experience to guide the motion planner towards planning goal. However, existing approaches often struggle to encode the spatial structure inherent in motion planning problems. To address this limitation, we introduce Graph-based Attention Masking for Spatial- and Embodiment-aware Motion Planning (GAIDE), a neural informed sampler that leverages both the spatial structure of the planning problem and the robotic manipulator's embodiment to guide the planning algorithm. GAIDE represents these structures as a graph and integrates it into a transformer-based neural sampler through attention masking. We evaluate GAIDE against baseline state-of-the-art sampling-based planners using uniform sampling, hand-crafted informed sampling, and neural informed sampling primitives. Evaluation results demonstrate that GAIDE improves planning efficiency and success rate.

### [37] [Act-Observe-Rewrite: Multimodal Coding Agents as In-Context Policy Learners for Robot Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04466)
*Vaishak Kumar*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: AOR框架利用多模态大语言模型，通过“执行-观察-重写”循环，在无需梯度更新、演示或奖励工程的情况下，让机器人通过合成新的Python代码来改进操作策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决多模态语言模型如何在没有外部监督（如梯度更新、示范数据或奖励设计）的情况下，通过推理自身失败来学习操纵物理物体的问题；旨在探索可解释代码作为策略表示如何带来不同于不透明神经策略的上下文学习能力。

Method: 提出Act-Observe-Rewrite (AOR) 框架：LLM智能体基于视觉观察和结构化的 episode 结果，在每次尝试之间完全自主地合成可执行的Python控制器代码；将底层电机控制实现作为LLM推理的基本单元，使智能体不仅能改变“做什么”，还能改变“怎么做”。

Result: 在三个robosuite操纵任务中验证了该方法，智能体无需演示、奖励工程或梯度更新即可实现高成功率，成功通过诊断系统性故障并重写其成因来提升策略。

Conclusion: 以可解释代码作为策略表示，能够赋予多模态语言模型独特的上下文学习能力，使其具备自我诊断和修正系统失败的能力，从而在无监督条件下实现有效的机器人操作策略进化。

Abstract: Can a multimodal language model learn to manipulate physical objects by reasoning about its own failures-without gradient updates, demonstrations, or reward engineering? We argue the answer is yes, under conditions we characterise precisely. We present Act-Observe-Rewrite (AOR), a framework in which an LLM agent improves a robot manipulation policy by synthesising entirely new executable Python controller code between trials, guided by visual observations and structured episode outcomes. Unlike prior work that grounds LLMs in pre-defined skill libraries or uses code generation for one-shot plan synthesis, AOR makes the full low-level motor control implementation the unit of LLM reasoning, enabling the agent to change not just what the robot does, but how it does it. The central claim is that interpretable code as the policy representation creates a qualitatively different kind of in-context learning from opaque neural policies: the agent can diagnose systematic failures and rewrite their causes. We validate this across three robosuite manipulation tasks and report promising results, with the agent achieving high success rates without demonstrations, reward engineering, or gradient updates.

</details>


### [38] [Efficient Autonomous Navigation of a Quadruped Robot in Underground Mines on Edge Hardware](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04470)
*Yixiang Gao,Kwame Awuah-Offei*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建了一个集成LiDAR-惯性里程计、基于先验地图的扫描匹配定位、地形分割、可见性图全局规划以及速度调节局部路径跟随器的导航栈；该系统无需特定环境训练或学习组件，仅需单次建图即可处理任意目标点。

Result: 在实验矿井中进行了20次重复试验（4个不同难度目标各5次），累计自主行走超过700米，成功率为100%，平均加权成功率(SPL)为0.73 ± 0.09，且保持了稳定的实时控制频率。

Abstract: Embodied navigation in underground mines faces significant challenges, including narrow passages, uneven terrain, near-total darkness, GPS-denied conditions, and limited communication infrastructure. While recent learning-based approaches rely on GPU-accelerated inference and extensive training data, we present a fully autonomous navigation stack for a Boston Dynamics Spot quadruped robot that runs entirely on a low-power Intel NUC edge computer with no GPU and no network connectivity requirements. The system integrates LiDAR-inertial odometry, scan-matching localization against a prior map, terrain segmentation, and visibility-graph global planning with a velocity-regulated local path follower, achieving real-time perception-to-action at consistent control rates. After a single mapping pass of the environment, the system handles arbitrary goal locations within the known map without any environment-specific training or learned components. We validate the system through repeated field trials using four target locations of varying traversal difficulty in an experimental underground mine, accumulating over 700 m of fully autonomous traverse with a 100% success rate across all 20 trials (5 repetitions x 4 targets) and an overall Success weighted by Path Length (SPL) of 0.73 \pm 0.09.
